<user>110956776127992967534< /user><review>(Translated by Google) I give 4 stars because I loved living down, the setting is super nice, a quarter of an hour walk or shuttle SDSU and the value for money compared to other residences is really worth it. There are many international students and the place makes it possible to make lots of meetings. The maintenance service is great and fast.
HOWEVER the big downside is the administrative service, if you arrive outside office hours, no one will be there to welcome you and give you the keys and you may end up on the street for the night. They will not give you any information, it's up to you to pick them up. Level payment of rent and deposit I think he should be ashamed. You have to pay to pay your rent and despite an impeccable apartment they will take you a nice sum on your deposit which will not be returned by transfer but thanks to a check sent to your home. To recover it do not be impatient and do not be afraid to contact them several times if you want to review the color ...
Mine is "weirdly" not arrived, result we must pay to have a follow-up to be sure that it is sent. Not to mention the cost of international calls that I had to make ...
To summarize, I recommend this residence which is for me the best but administrative side I think they are thieves and there is much progress to be made.

First time here for me.  Was staying in town and wanted something to drink.  It isn't the fanciest place for sure, but their prices are reasonable and they have a pretty good selection.  Oddly, they also sell a number of other things making it a bit of a mini-mart.  The guy behind the counter was very friendly and helpful.  I was quite happy with my purchase.</review>

<review>My husband and I live around the corner from this place and have been staring at the "Coming Soon" sign for a while now, patiently waiting for the doors to open.

Well, last night as I was out fetching Panda Express for the kiddos, I noticed that the "Coming Soon" sign had changed to "Now Open."

I shouldn't have stopped.  I should have waited for my husband to get back from working out of town.  I should have resisted the urge to give the place a try.... oh, but I'm glad I didn't.

Let's talk basics...

The digs:  So, yes. This little restaurant is located in a strip mall next to a shoe store.  Don't hold that against them.  Once you walk inside, you will see that the place is bright and clean and the epitome of minimalistic class.  No gawdy decor, no loud music; just clean, bright and simple.

The peeps:  Upon entering, I was greeted by a friendly young gentleman who answered all of my questions about the menu items, made a suggestion (spicy chicken plate), and then seated me in a booth.  As I waited for the food to be prepared, the same gentleman brought me a delicious piece of petra cake that I enjoyed while I waited.  A young woman who was tidying up after a previous customer also greeted me kindly.  Overall, at this point, the people were the best part of the place so far.... that was, of course, until I tasted the food.

The grub:  They get it.  I mean, they really get it. It was a perfect marriage of subtle spice and inviting seasonings.  The chicken was tender, but not mushy. The salad, the hummus, the garlic sauce and pita bread... all good.  And the rice!  Yum.  As I mentioned previously, my whole mission before my visit to Petra was to pick up Panda for my children, so I had to take my food to go.  Let's just put it this way, all three of my children no longer had any interest in their chain-created mock-chinese food; They wanted mine instead.  Even my 13 year old son, who swears he's the next Gordon Ramsey, gave it a rave review.

In conclusion, this place is definitely worthy of a 5 star rating.  I can't wait to try all the different plates and dishes.   We definitely needed a good Mediterranean restaurant around here, and Petra delivers the goods.

Go check them out. You will not be disappointed.  üòÄ<//review><Rate>5</Rate>< gmapID>

< Text>
Who wouldn't love to see the end of Route 66??  I know I Love it and have loved it for over 4 decades!!
What other road ANYWHERE in the world will play 'America The Beautiful'? While your pondering that, how many roads do you know extend over 2,400 miles??  How about a road that has been in existence for nearly a Century???  You'll find that all, on Route 66!!  As far as the end of it, well, the only reason it ended, is because there was no more land to continue it.  Do yourself a favor, if you ever find yourself bored, or have nothing better to do, take a ride to The End of Route 66!!  You'll thank me later.  Route 66 is truly 'The Stuff of Legend!'< /Text>

< review>
Just finished up visiting. Dad is a HUGE John Force fan, hes visiting from NY and 1 of the places he wanted to go while out visiting was John Forces museum. As someone else mentioned, museum is $5 bucks but they give u $5 off when u spend $30. Good deal IMHO especially since in the store everything is reasonably priced. That being said the 3 people we dealt with at Racestation today 8/25 in the afternoon were AMAZING. Beyond friendly and courteous. With the amount of Force racing memorabilia in the museum it was worth the $5. Its awe inspiring to see so many of the trophies he won there. But the people here were amazing, knowledgeable and courteous and they put on a good face for the Force organization. It is well worth a stop to view, weather you are a huge fan like my dad is or a casual fan like myself.<//review>

{'time': 1620752025488, 'text': 'Thank you, We appreciate your star rating and would like to discuss how we can improve your service experience. Please send an email to socialsupport@terminix.com listing details of your experience, full service address and the phone number associated with the account.'}</resp>
< text>
I'm trying to cancel all 3 services I have with Terminix due ONLY to their inept customer service.  The technicians I've had the pleasure to work with have been fabulous - courteous, professional, responsive and very effective.  They go the extra mile when asked for help. I've been with Terminix for something like 15 years at 2 different addresses in different parts of the US.  If it was just on the strength of the technicians I would recommend Terminix unreservedly with 5 stars.

That's why cancelling my services is so painful, because I know there are hard-working, dedicated professionals who work there.

Unfortunately the customer service or account administration is woeful.  This includes billing and just getting to a person that can help (that is not a technician).  As I write this, I have been on hold for 35 minutes trying to reach someone in the "cancellation department" to cancel my services.

Here follows a more detailed description of the sad state of Terminix's customer support in my case.

For the 1st 2 months of 2021, I got no invoices from Terminix for my termite protection services.  I called Terminix in January to try and understand what was going on, but all the people I spoke to could not understand what was going on either.  Call-backs that were promised never happened.  Finally in March I got 3 months worth of invoices in 1 invoice that simply said I was past due.  No explanation or apology, and I was made to feel responsible for what turned out to be an  invoicing issue at Terminix that affected a lot of customers.

My next invoices in April had a 6% price increase across the board.  No explanation was given and no warning.  I talked to several phone reps about the increase.  They all promised call backs from the "local" office that never materialised.  The last rep I spoke to said that it was an oversight and that the original charge amount was correct and would be reinstated.  Again, he said he was filing this with the local office who would contact me. Nothing happened, and the charges stayed the same.

When I called back, a different rep sent an email to the local branch service manager to ask for follow-up.  (I know this because I saw a copy of her email).  The local branch service manager then sent me an email with the data he had scraped from Zillow about my house and said that since my house was worth so much money that paying Terminix seemed "pretty low for a house of that value".

Caifornia is not known for cheap real estate, so I pointed out to him that the cost to rebuild the house is a fraction of the "value" he had pulled off Zillow.  Most of the value is in the land.

This same person then took a different tack and told me by email that they had to increase rates due to increases in cost.  When I asked why there was no notice and why this increase was not aligned with the contract renewal (as required in my contract), I got radio silence.

After about a week, I called again, and this time was called back by another "local" rep.  I couldn't take the call and it went to voice mail where he left me a call-back number.  I called that number within a few hours and left him a voice mail message inviting him to call me.  Now several days later, there has been no response.

So here I am, very frustrated by the ineffectiveness of my efforts to understand (and help) Terminix's billing and customer service process, and unwilling to be disrespected by their "local" customer service any more.  I will be sending my technician an email saying how sorry I am to be parting company and thank him for everything he has done for me.

I hope if you have made it this far, you have found this review helpful.

PS It took 50 minutes to connect with someone who could help me cancel my contracts.  She was super friendly and very apologetic, and is a great example of what good customer service can be.  Terminix could use more people like her.< /text>

<rating>4<//rating>< text>
My score isn't related to associate/service, but the approach. When I first met with a sales associate and they inspected my home back in 2010 they didn't find any live termites, but said I had termites because they found wood damage and termite droppings even though another company a year prior when I bought the home gave termite clearance report. The past several years during inspections and when I've been doing work to the house I continue to find wood damage, further deterioration, and termite pellets. Now that I have paid double what most companies charge to have my house tented and my annual $250 policy renewal they say that I don't have termites no matter what they see/find and indicate basically I would have to start chopping apart wood to try find live termites. This methodology is not consistent and deceptive. If a house doesn't have termites unless they find live bugs, that should be the litmus test on all inspections including before signing sales contract or buying/selling a home. Now due to all the termite damage most of my decks have progressed with wood rot. So basically I feel that the warranty and protection plan doesn't really do much and is not consistent. This is a systemic company wide issue as this methodology has been projected by every tech except the original tech who sold us on tenting the house and termite protection plan.<//text>
